Create a react app with a dashboard that includes graphs like gauges and timegraphs as well as a chatbot. The graphs will update in real time and recieve continuous data from  an api gateway. Here is the Architecture Document for context: # **IIoT Application Architecture + AI Assistant with AWS and GPT Actions** * Data is sent via **HTTP POST**. * Data includes: `timestamp`, `sensor_id`, `sensor_value`, etc. ### **2. Amazon API Gateway (HTTP API)** * Exposes a secure HTTP endpoint to receive data from devices. * Connects directly to a Lambda function. * Method: `POST /ingest` ### **3. AWS Lambda (Ingestor)** * Functionality: Receive data from the API Gateway and publish it to **Kinesis Data Streams**. * Validates and transforms data if needed. ### **4. Amazon Kinesis Data Streams** * Real-time streaming system. * Receives events from the Lambda Ingestor. * Redirects data to an external schema in the serverless Redshift database. ### **5. Amazon Redshift Serverless** * Relational analytical database. * Stores sensor time series data. * Data is available from a materialized view of the schema. * Supports complex SQL queries. ### **6. Amazon API Gateway (for frontend)** * Exposes a second set of routes for the frontend to query historical or real-time data from Redshift. * Connects to Lambda, which executes SQL and returns results in JSON format. * Method: `POST /query` ### **7. Query Lambda** * Receives requests from the frontend with filters (date, sensor_id, etc.). * Executes SQL queries in Redshift. * Returns structured results for graphing or other visualizations. ## **AI Assistant with GPT Actions** ### **8. Frontend (AI Chat)** * A chat interface where the user asks questions such as: "What was the maximum temperature recorded by sensor S1 yesterday?" * Sends: * The question * User ID * Necessary variables or context * Via: * **API Gateway** → **Lambda IA** ### **6. Amazon API Gateway (for AI)** * Exposes a third set of routes for the frontend to ask the AI assistant about information in the Redshift database. * Receives the user's question along with context such as the user ID and the variable being asked about. * Connects to the Lambda IA, which transfers the question and context to the GPT action. * Method: `POST /ask` ### **9. Lambda IA** * Receives questions and context from the API Gateway. * Calls a **custom GPT Action** with the obtained information. * Receives the enriched response in natural language and returns it to the frontend via API Gateway. ### **10. GPT Action (OpenAI)** * Interprets the natural language question. * Generates the corresponding SQL based on the question and context. * Sends the SQL to the Middleware Lambda function to execute the query in Redshift. * Receives the query result from the Lambda function and generates the enriched response. * Returns the enriched response to Lambda IA. ## **Complete Data Flow** ### **1. IIoT Ingestion** ``` ESP32 → API Gateway (/ingest) → Lambda Ingestor → Kinesis Data Stream → Redshift Serverless ``` ### **2. Query from Frontend** ``` Frontend → API Gateway (/query) → Query Lambda → SQL to Redshift → Returns JSON results ``` ### **3. AI Assistant** ``` Frontend → API Gateway (/ask) → Lambda IA → GPT Action - Generates SQL → Lambda Middleware - SQL in Redshift → GPT Action - Receives data and responds → Lambda IA → Frontend ```
